<p><b>ве́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>сить</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-вес-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вес.html>вес</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ves</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веский.html>ве́ский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">véskij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ве́сче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>weighty, heavy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> substantial, significant, serious</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> convincing, persuasive <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of an argument or reason</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вес.html>ве́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кий.html>кий</a></b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веский.html>ве́ский</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">véskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:весло.html>весло́</a> (4177)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:весло.html>весло́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">veslo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*veslo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">oar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весло.html>весло́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vesló</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весло.html>весла́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весло.html>вёсла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весло.html>вёсел</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>oar, paddle, scull</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal  slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> spoon</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rifle, especially a sniper rifle (which looks like an oar)</li></ol>

***веснушка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:веснушка.html>весну́шка</a> (12231)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">весну́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vesnúxa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">freckle; fever</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Per Vasmer, the original meaning of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">весну́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vesnúxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> was approximately "spring disease", from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весна.html>весна́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vesná</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веснушка.html>весну́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vesnúška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веснушка.html>весну́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веснушка.html>весну́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веснушка.html>весну́шек</a></b>)
</p>

***вести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести</a> (306)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vesti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>повести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lead, to preside over, to chair
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заседание.html>заседа́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vestí</b> zasedánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to preside over a meeting</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:переговоры.html>перегово́ры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vestí</b> peregovóry</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to negotiate, to conduct negotiations</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vestí sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to behave like</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плохо.html>пло́хо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">plóxo sebjá <b>vestí</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to behave poorly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vestí</b> sebjá xorošó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to acquit oneself well</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to drive</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_3">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></b> is a concrete verb. Its counterpart, <a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a>, is an abstract verb.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вес.html>вес</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 7b/b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>повести</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начальный.html>нача́льной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рме</a> омофоничен <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a>. ***вестись.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вестись.html>вести́сь</a> (4084)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вестись.html>вести́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vestísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повестись.html>повести́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li>to be in progress, to be underway
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вестись.html>веду́тся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:исследование.html>иссле́дования</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́лью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:создание.html>созда́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теория.html>тео́рии</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vedútsja</b> isslédovanija s célʹju sozdánija nóvoj teórii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Efforts are underway toward the construction of a new theory</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вестись.html>веду́тся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:переговоры.html>перегово́ры</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> безви́зовом <a href = vnd.unilang:режим.html>режи́ме</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vedútsja</b> peregovóry o bezvízovom režíme.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The visa-free talks are underway.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be conducted, to be carried on, to be observed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>Так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уж.html>уж</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вестись.html>ведётся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tak už u nas <b>vedjótsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">That's a custom among us</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to yield, to succumb, to give in (to somebody's) lies, to provocation, etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вестись.html>веди́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:провокация.html>провока́ции</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne <b>vedísʹ</b> na jevó provokácii.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Don't give in to his provocations (i.e. "Don't be fooled by his provocations").</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вес.html>вес</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ти́сь</b>

***весь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a> (24390)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vьśь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vesʹ</span>) (<i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>вся</a></b>, <i>neuter</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a></b>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>all, the whole, the whole of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vesʹ</b> denʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">all day; all day long</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязный.html>гря́зный</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vesʹ</b> grjáznyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dirty all over, all dirty</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снегу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vesʹ</b> v snegú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">covered with snow</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vsevó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in all; altogether; sum total</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́шего</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vsevó xoróševo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">all the best; good luck</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">лу́чше <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lúčše vsevó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">best of all</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всём</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́ре</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vo <b>vsjóm</b> míre</i> ― <span class="e-translation">all over the world</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изо.html>и́зо</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всех</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ízo <b>vsex</b> sil</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with all one’s might</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всей</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:страна.html>стране́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>vsej</b> strané</i> ― <span class="e-translation">throughout the country</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всём</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>том</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pri <b>vsjóm</b> tom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for all that</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>everything, all</li>
<li>everybody, everyone</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vesʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and its various forms can be used both as adjectives and as pronouns. As adjectives, the forms of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vesʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> correspond roughly to the English adjectives <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">all</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">every</i>. When used as pronouns, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vse</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> means <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">everyone</i>, and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vsjo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> means <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">everything</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">all</i>. For example,
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиди́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:компьютер.html>компью́тером</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On sidít za kompʹjútɛrom <b>vesʹ</b> denʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He sits at the computer <b>all</b> day.</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:съесть.html>съе́ли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>еду́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní sʺjéli <b>vsju</b> jedú.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They ate <b>all</b> the food.</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обойти.html>обошли́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:магазин.html>магази́ны</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My obošlí <b>vse</b> magazíny.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We went to <b>all</b> the stores.</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почти.html>почти́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:концерт.html>конце́рте</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Počtí <b>vse</b> býli na koncérte.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><i>Almost <b>everyone</b> was at the concert.</i></span></div></li>

***ветвь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветвь.html>ветвь</a> (3303)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вѣтвь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">větvĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">ве́тва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vétva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветка.html>ве́тка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vétka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:веять.html>ве́я</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">véja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">вейка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vejka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">vȇja</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">větev</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">vetva</i>. Non-Slavic cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vītis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Weide</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">willow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Prussian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Prussian language">Old Prussian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="prg">witwan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">willow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">بید</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bid</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">willow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветвь.html>ветвь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vetvʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветвь.html>ве́тви</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветвь.html>ве́тви</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветвь.html>ветве́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>branch, bough, limb (woody part of a tree arising from the trunk and usually dividing)</li></ol>

***ветер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ветер</a> (485)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*větrъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂weh₁-</i>.
Compare to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wetter</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">weather</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">véter</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тры</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ветра́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ветро́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тров</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Poetic.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">meteorology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wind</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">plural only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the wind(s), flatus</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the wave of change <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually in the phrase <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:перемена.html>переме́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><b>véter</b> peremén</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветка.html>ветка</a> (1923)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветка.html>ве́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vétka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветка.html>ве́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветка.html>ве́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветка.html>ве́ток</a></b>)

***ветхий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветхий.html>ве́тхий</a> (9308)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ветъхъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vetŭxŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vetъxъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">old, ancient</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветхий.html>ве́тхий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vétxij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ве́тше</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ancient, old
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветхий.html>ве́тхий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завет.html>заве́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vétxij Zavét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Old Testament</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>old, dilapidated, shabby, ramshackle, decrepit, rickety</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вече.html>ве́че</a> (32378)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вѣче</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">věče</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*věťe</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вече.html>ве́че</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">véče</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вече.html>ве́ча</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вече.html>ве́ча</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вече.html>ве́ч</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вече.html>ве́чей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> veche (a <a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a> assembly in medieval Slavic countries).</li></ol>

***вечер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>вечер</a> (234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*večerъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wekʷsperos</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἕσπερος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hésperos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vesper</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">գիշեր</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gišer</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>ве́чер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">véčer</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>ве́чера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>вечера́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>вечеро́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>evening (after 8 PM)</li>
<li>tonight, this evening
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>ве́чер</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обещать.html>обеща́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приятный.html>прия́тным</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Véčer</b> obeščájet bytʹ prijátnym.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Tonight is going to be a pleasant night.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> party, social gathering, soiree</li></ol>
